name:M‚Äçi‚Äçl‚Äçl‚Äçi‚Äçe‚ÄçW‚Äço‚Äçn‚Äçg
info:Garden Deluxe Family Friendly Suite
info:Stayed in August 2022
info:Family
info:1 Review
rating:5
posted:Posted August 20, 2022
msg:There are some surprises in China Life Jiayuan. I thought it was a homestay based on the name, but I didn't expect it to be a serious 4üåü hotel.
From the layout, interior, and hotel environment, the room can be obtained by seeing the reservation picture.
The room has a layout of two rooms and two living rooms, 120 square meters, large enough and spacious, and equipped with a kitchen, which is especially suitable for family travel and more suitable for long-term rental.
Soft clothing is also quite tasteful. The overall color uses Tiffany blue + white and Chinese furniture, and there is a tatami in the back hall, which can be used as a living room or a study.
The bedding materials are very particular, and the first night I didn't have insomnia because I didn't recognize the bed.
The bath water is big and comfortable.
Change and wash 4 sets of towels are thick and clean.
There is also an outdoor swimming pool and an internet celebrity surfing pool. The 15-minute surfing is included in the room rate, of course, it is not included in the extended stay.
The breakfast is flawless, but the room includes 4 breakfasts (a waste of one per day) is quite cost-effective. Buy 58/bit alone.
If I had to say a disadvantage, it might be,
1. The toilet is not smart;
2. The gym facilities are a bit rudimentary, a treadmill and a pool table are placed together, which is strange;
3. The surrounding facilities are not perfect, there are many projects under construction, not to mention eating and shopping.

The night view of the hotel is good, be bold, go to the place where there are no lights in the hotel at night, you can see fireflies.

During the silent period, according to the policy at the time, the extended stay will be calculated at half price of the original order. However, the dine-in was suspended, the breakfast became a bento box, and the 58/person was downgraded to 25/person; the swimming pool and wave pool were gradually suspended;
More than less than above. At that time, we had no problem eating. The hotel had a guaranteed car that was in charge of purchasing, and we could have hot lunches for breakfast, including porridge, yogurt, and milk. There was room-service for lunch and dinner. 58/piece still has fruit, no price increase, it's a conscience price. It is said that at that time, people who lived in B&Bs began to choose group leaders for group purchases.

We are also actively coordinating with the Prevention and Control Office, so that we boarded the plane back to Shanghai as soon as the quiet period on 8.13 came.

Above, if I have the opportunity to come to Haitang Bay in Sanya, China Life Jiayuan is still my first choice.
